<h3 class="hidden">Choose the language</h3>

Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h1 to h3

Don't skip heading levels. Use h2 instead of h3

<button aria-label="toppmeny" class="hamburger" tabindex="0"> <span class="hamburger__line"></span> <span class="hamburger__line"></span> <span class="hamburger__line"></span> </button>
